### 8. Hacking & Security & News
- [Online Spyware Watchdog](http://spywareitdaiuyfo2sqb5vsg7mek5cjabdr73luhnda57t2hyuzg7yyd.onion/) - `http://spywareitdaiuyfo2sqb5vsg7mek5cjabdr73luhnda57t2hyuzg7yyd.onion/`
> The goal of this website is to classify spyware programs, so that users can be more aware that they are installing spyware.This site can help you to fight against surveillance.
- [CryptBB](http://cryptbbtg65gibadeeo2awe3j7s6evg7eklserehqr4w4e2bis5tebid.onion/) - `http://cryptbbtg65gibadeeo2awe3j7s6evg7eklserehqr4w4e2bis5tebid.onion/`
> CryptBB is an advanced Cyber Security and Hacking Forum powered by LongPig and Power, it's been on Tor since 2017.
CryptBB focuses on security and anonymity by offering customized security measures to all users and a secure environment where users can discuss and trade in total security, anonymity and privacy.
- [MAT2- Remove Metadata](http://liqr2cbsjzxmpw6savgh274tuzl34x6cd56h7m7ceatnrokveffm66ad.onion/) - `http://liqr2cbsjzxmpw6savgh274tuzl34x6cd56h7m7ceatnrokveffm66ad.onion/`
> The file you see is just the tip of the iceberg. MetaData is just a small amount of data that is hidden inside you files and multimedia. (Location, Date of creation, Last edit, System info ). With the help of this DarkNet site you can remove that hidden metadata from your files.
- [Quantum Blog](http://quantum445bh3gzuyilxdzs5xdepf3b7lkcupswvkryf3n7hgzpxebid.onion/) - `http://quantum445bh3gzuyilxdzs5xdepf3b7lkcupswvkryf3n7hgzpxebid.onion/`
> Quantum Blog inform the society about attacks and consequences, about information leaked to the hackers. All databases are completely free, available for all visitors to download, use and repost in any place.
- [Breachdb Database Search Engine](http://breachdbsztfykg2fdaq2gnqnxfsbj5d35byz3yzj73hazydk4vq72qd.onion) - `http://breachdbsztfykg2fdaq2gnqnxfsbj5d35byz3yzj73hazydk4vq72qd.onion`
> Breachdb is a dark net website where you can search a username or email and get info that the given username are available in a data breach or not. They also had a huge collection of de-hashed passwords.

### 12. File Host
- [Turbo](http://3qeyzgtujhguzjletcz34qxsiqoymlni6s6rhc37kpobyttzngwlzjid.onion/) - `http://3qeyzgtujhguzjletcz34qxsiqoymlni6s6rhc37kpobyttzngwlzjid.onion/`
> Turbo is a DarkNet free secure file hosting where you can upload your file and send via p2p service or upload up-to 300mb file directly to the server to get the share and delete links. File will be stored for maximum 40 days. Site will also delete exIf (meta data) from media files (JPG, PDF, PSD, E.T.C). You can also share notes to anyone and note will be automatically deleted once they view it.
